--
-- Table structure for table `sponsor_t`
--

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `sponsor_t`;
CREATE TABLE `sponsor_t` (
  `SPONSOR_ID` decimal(10,0) NOT NULL default '0',
  `SPONSOR_NAME` varchar(150) NOT NULL default '',
  `SPONSOR_ALL_LEVELS` varchar(100) default NULL,
  `SPONSOR_LEVEL_1` varchar(30) default NULL,
  `SPONSOR_LEVEL_2` varchar(30) default NULL,
  `SPONSOR_LEVEL_3` varchar(30) default NULL,
  `SPONSOR_ABBREVIATION` varchar(30) default NULL,
  `SPONSOR_ORIGIN` varchar(20) default NULL,
  `SPONSOR_FUND_SOURCE` varchar(30) default NULL,
  `SPONSOR_EMAIL_ADDRESS` varchar(50) default NULL,
  `SPONSOR_WEB_SITE` varchar(100) default NULL,
  `SPONSOR_STREET_1` varchar(60) default NULL,
  `SPONSOR_STREET_2` varchar(60) default NULL,
  `SPONSOR_CITY` varchar(40) default NULL,
  `SPONSOR_STATE` varchar(20) default NULL,
  `SPONSOR_COUNTRY` varchar(30) default NULL,
  `SPONSOR_ZIP_CODE` varchar(20) default NULL,
  `SPONSOR_LEVEL` char(2) default NULL,
